+ outer_baffle(s) + inner_baffle(s)<br>28) full_PFR_wall : outer_PFR__wall(s) + inner_PFR_wall(s)<br>29) core_cut_X2 : y-aligned edges inside the separatrix connecting to the non-active x-point<br>30)
